# Changelog

Wszystkie istotne zmiany w Ghost Empire sńÖ opisane w tym pliku.

Format opiera sińô na [Keep a Changelog](https://keepachangelog.com/en/1.1.0/).
Wersje datowane (kalendarzowe) zamiast SemVer ‚ÄĒ projekt jest aplikacjńÖ, nie bibliotekńÖ.

## [Unreleased]

### Changed

- **`/polls` and `/predictions` tally via `groupBy` instead of loading every row (audit v4 perf)** **(#635)** ‚ÄĒ both public pages loaded **all** vote/entry rows and counted in JS: `/polls` pulled every `PollVote` for 30 polls each render; `/predictions` pulled every `PredictionEntry` (unbounded) for active predictions to sum wagers. A popular poll/prediction made these heavy index-less reads on every page load. Now both use DB aggregation (`pollVote.groupBy [pollId,optionIndex] _count`; `predictionEntry.groupBy [predictionId,optionIndex] _sum+_count`) + a small scoped fetch of only the viewer's own votes/entries ‚ÄĒ exactly what the OBS overlay feeds already did. Output payload shape is byte-identical, so the client components are unchanged. Index-backed (`[pollId,optionIndex]`, `[predictionId,optionIndex]` exist). No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/`eslint`/`build`/`docs:check`.

- **Donation poll every 15 min instead of once a day (audit v4 perf)** **(#634)** ‚ÄĒ `/api/cron/streamlabs-poll` ran `0 6 * * *` (once daily), so a Streamlabs donation could wait **up to ~24h** before crediting GT + firing the thank-you ‚ÄĒ brutal for a live-stream economy. Now `*/15 * * * *` (every 15 min). The handler is cheap and idempotent (dedup via `Donation.externalId @unique`), so the higher cadence can't double-credit. Requires Vercel **Pro** (sub-daily crons) ‚ÄĒ confirmed by the owner. Config-only. Zielone: `build`/`docs:check`.

### Fixed

- **Docs refresh + owner runbook (audit v4)** **(#636)** ‚ÄĒ closed the documentation drift the audit found: **ROADMAP** ‚ÄĒ struck the two stale "do zrobienia" items already shipped (`@simplewebauthn` 9‚Üí13 #629, reactCompiler‚ÜĒeslint #617) and added a fresh "ŇöwieŇľo dowiezione" wave for #618‚Äď#635; **ENV.md** ‚ÄĒ documented `AUTH_URL` (the Auth.js-v5 alias that takes precedence and that passkeys pin rpID/origin to); **ARCHITECTURE.md ¬ß9** ‚ÄĒ added the per-tenant game-library models (`Game.tenantId` #618, `GameVote` #628, `GameLibraryConfig.psnNpsso`/`xboxApiKey` #626/#627); **new `docs/OWNER-SETUP.md`** ‚ÄĒ one consolidated checklist for the owner-only actions previously scattered across docs (Game backfill, PSN/Xbox key setup + live test, passkey device test, dedicated prod `ENCRYPTION_KEY`, raffle-bot wiring, infra hygiene). Docs-only. Zielone: `docs:check`.

- **CHANGELOG repair + docs:check gap-detection (audit v4)** **(#633)** ‚ÄĒ restored two entries whose bold titles had been clobbered when later entries were prepended, leaving orphaned bodies with no PR reference: **#629** (`@simplewebauthn` 9‚Üí13) and **#631** (admin `secDesc_*`). Root cause: `docs:check` only compared the **highest** PR number, so an intermediate gap (e.g. #629 missing while #630 was present) passed green. Hardened `scripts/check-docs-sync.mjs` to verify **every** PR referenced in recent git history appears in the CHANGELOG, not just the max ‚ÄĒ the gap that hid #629 can't recur. Docs/tooling only. Zielone: `tsc`/`eslint`/`build`/`docs:check`.
- **Game-vote tally was aggregated across all portals in the null-tenant path (audit v4)** **(#632)** ‚ÄĒ on `/games` the "play next" vote tally used `where: { ...(tid ? { tenantId } : {}) }`, so when no tenant resolved (`tid` null) the `where` was **empty** and counted **every portal's** votes globally ‚ÄĒ inconsistent with `myVote`, which correctly scoped to `{ tenantId: null }`. Latent today (single live portal) but a cross-portal leak the moment a second portal exists before subdomain resolution is wired. Now the tally matches `myVote`: `tid ? { tenantId: tid } : { tenantId: null }`. The vote write path (`/api/games/vote`) was already correctly scoped. One-line scoping fix, no schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/`eslint`/`build`/`docs:check`.

- **Admin section descriptions showed a raw i18n key (audit v4)** **(#631)** ‚ÄĒ 13 admin sections (`recap`, `clipdirector`, `economy`, `payments`, `notifications`, `sponsors`, `collectibles`, `community`, `clanwars`, `trivia`, `twofactor`, `scenes`, `soundrewards`) had no `secDesc_*` translation, so opening e.g. `/admin#payments` literally rendered the string `admin.secDesc_payments` in the help banner. Added all 13 keys (EN + PL) in the friendly explanatory style of the existing ones. UI-only, no code/schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/`eslint`/`build`/`docs:check`.

### Changed

- **Regression tests for the season-rollover math (audit v3 hygiene)** **(#630)** ‚ÄĒ closes the last named test gap from the audit's Wave 5: the monthly Battle Pass rollover core, `seasons.monthBounds`, was untested. Exported it (pure; zero behavior change) and added **6 tests** locking in the UTC month window, the season **number from the Jan-2026 epoch** (Jan 2026 = 1, +12/year, December's end rolling into the next year) and the Polish month label ‚ÄĒ the off-by-one-prone bits. Audited the rest of the money/progression pure logic (`economy.ts` payouts/duel-rake/heist-odds/tiers/level+prestige multipliers/discounts) and confirmed it's **already fully covered** (no new gaps). **468 tests** total. No prod code path changed. Zielone: `tsc`/**468 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.

- **`@simplewebauthn` 9 ‚Üí 13 (passkeys, audit v3 hygiene)** **(#629)** ‚ÄĒ bumped `@simplewebauthn/server` + `/browser` four majors to **v13.3.1** and adapted the 4 passkey routes + 2 client calls to the new API: `userID` is now a `Uint8Array`, credential ids are **base64url strings** (not Buffers) in `excludeCredentials`/`verifyAuthenticationResponse`, the verify result moved to `registrationInfo.credential.{id,publicKey,counter}`, the auth verifier takes `credential` (was `authenticator`), the deprecated `@simplewebauthn/types` imports moved to `@simplewebauthn/server`, and the browser `startRegistration`/`startAuthentication` now take `{ optionsJSON }`. **Done before passkeys' first real device test on purpose** ‚ÄĒ there are ~no stored credentials yet, so the upcoming test validates v13 directly (no v9‚Üív13 credential-format migration to worry about). Passkeys remain **isolated from OAuth** (a passkey issue can never break OAuth sign-in) and still **need the live device test** before being relied on (unchanged status). `next-auth` keeps a *peerOptional* `@simplewebauthn/server@^9` for its (unused) WebAuthn provider ‚ÄĒ cosmetic warning, verified harmless by a green `build`. tsc verifies the whole adaptation against the installed v13 types. Zielone: `tsc`/**462 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.

### Added

- **"Vote for the next game" on the library (audit v3)** **(#628)** ‚ÄĒ the capstone on the now-complete per-tenant game library (Steam+PSN+Xbox): logged-in viewers **pick ONE game per portal** they want the streamer to play next, right on `/games`. Each card gets a ūüĎć vote count + a "Play next / Voted" button, and the leader is highlighted with a **ūüŹÜ Most-wanted** ring. New `GameVote` model (**db push** ‚ÄĒ new table, per-tenant, `@@unique([userId, tenantId])` = one active pick per viewer, cascade on game prune). `POST /api/games/vote` (auth, rate-limited, tenant-scoped, validates the game is a visible game of this portal) **moves the single vote atomically** (delete-then-create) or clears it; the button `router.refresh()`es so counts stay consistent when a vote moves. Free (no GT). EN + PL. Zielone: `tsc`/**462 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Per-portal Xbox connect (audit v3 white-label)** **(#627)** ‚ÄĒ completes the "connect your own game platforms" trilogy (Steam + PSN #626 + **Xbox**): each streamer can sync their **Xbox / Game Pass played-titles** library via an **OpenXBL (`xbl.io`) API key** (the pragmatic alternative to Microsoft's partner-gated XSAPI ‚ÄĒ no new dependency, plain `fetch`). New `GameLibraryConfig.xboxApiKey` (**db push** ‚ÄĒ additive nullable, applied) stores the key **encrypted at rest** (AES-256-GCM via `lib/crypto`; never returned to the client). A masked write-only field + Save + Sync in `/admin#games`; pure `lib/xbox` (`mapXboxTitles` ‚ÄĒ defensive title/image mapping, **+4 tests ‚Üí 462**) + `syncXboxLibrary` (per-portal key, tenant-scoped upsert/prune like Steam/PSN, `xboxSyncedAt`). **Ships dormant** ‚ÄĒ activates once a streamer pastes their xbl.io key; **needs a live test with a real key** (the OpenXBL schema can't be exercised locally). No new route (actions on the existing admin endpoint). EN + PL. Zielone: `tsc`/**462 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Per-portal PSN connect (audit v3 white-label)** **(#626)** ‚ÄĒ completes the per-tenant game library (#618): each streamer can now connect **their own PlayStation account** instead of sharing one global env token. New `GameLibraryConfig.psnNpsso` (**db push** ‚ÄĒ additive nullable, applied) stores the portal's **NPSSO encrypted at rest** (AES-256-GCM via `lib/crypto`; never returned to the client ‚ÄĒ the admin only sees a "set/not set" state). A masked write-only field + Save in `/admin#games`; the PSN sync now resolves the **per-portal NPSSO first, then the global `PSN_NPSSO` env as back-compat fallback**, and stamps a per-portal `psnSyncedAt`. `fetchPsnTitles(npsso)` takes the token as a param (no longer reads the env directly). **Xbox connect is still greenfield** (no integration exists yet) ‚ÄĒ tracked separately. No new route (a `set_psn_npsso` action on the existing admin endpoint). EN + PL. Zielone: `tsc`/**458 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Raffle bot integration runbook** **(#625)** ‚ÄĒ documents the exact contract the sibling `ghost-empire-chat` bot must implement to activate the chat-keyword raffle (shipped dormant in #611/#615): poll `raffleKeywords` from `GET /api/bot/chat-commands` (public, Host-scoped), then POST each chat hit to `POST /api/internal/raffle-entry` (Bearer `BOT_SECRET`, body `{ keyword, platform, username, isSub, isMod }`) ‚ÄĒ with the response contract, ticket-weight rules, local-dedupe guidance and a copy-paste reference snippet. New `docs/RAFFLE-BOT.md`. Docs-only, no code change. Zielone: `docs:check`.
- **Admin-list search in Collectibles (audit v3 UX)** **(#624)** ‚ÄĒ extends #620/#622 to the collectible-cards manager (`/admin#collectibles`): the search box (shown once the catalog passes 8 cards) filters by name/description/rarity **before** the cards are grouped by rarity, so only matching rarity groups render. Reuses the diacritic-insensitive, token-AND `lib/list-filter`; client-only, no API/schema change, no new tests. Zielone: `tsc`/**458 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Per-portal background templates (audit v3 white-label)** **(#623)** ‚ÄĒ instead of hunting for and pasting an image URL, a streamer can now pick a ready-made **dark gradient background** for their portal in `/admin#tenants` (a swatch picker: Nebula / Ember / Forest / Abyss / Plum / Aurora, plus "None" and the existing custom-URL field). **No schema change** ‚ÄĒ the choice is stored in the existing `Tenant.bgImageUrl` via a `preset:<id>` scheme: the read path (`tenant.ts`) resolves a known preset to its CSS gradient (exposed as `bgPreset`) and otherwise treats the value as a sanitized image URL; the layout applies the gradient directly (presets are dark by design, so contrast is preserved without an overlay). The preset id is allowlist-checked on both read and the admin write path (so it survives `safeMediaUrl`, which only passes http(s)). Pure `lib/bg-presets` (`isBgPreset`/`bgPresetId`/`resolveBgPresetCss`, **+4 tests ‚Üí 458**). EN + PL. Zielone: `tsc`/**458 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Admin-list search extended to commands / FAQ / events (audit v3 UX)** **(#622)** ‚ÄĒ follows #620: the reusable `ListSearch` + `lib/list-filter` primitive is now also wired into **Chat commands** (by trigger/response), **FAQ** (by keyword/response) and **Events** (by name/type), each showing the search box once the list passes 8 rows. Same diacritic-insensitive, token-AND matching; client-only, no API/schema change, no new tests (reuses the #620 lib). Zielone: `tsc`/**454 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **"View portal as a viewer" preview mode (audit v3 UX)** **(#621)** ‚ÄĒ an owner/mod can now flip the portal into a **viewer's-eye view** to QA the public experience: a toggle in the account menu (**"View as viewer"**) hides the admin/mod chrome (the **ADMIN/MOD header badges**) and shows a sticky amber **banner** with one-click exit. It's a **purely cosmetic lens** persisted in a cookie (`ge-view-as-viewer`, read server-side in the layout so there's no first-paint flash) ‚ÄĒ **it never relaxes a permission** (the server still gates `/admin` and every admin API), so it's safe by design. New `ViewerPreviewProvider`/`useViewerPreview` context + `ViewerPreviewBanner`, wired through `Providers` and the `Header`. Pure `lib/viewer-preview` (cookie parse/serialize, **+5 tests ‚Üí 454**). No API/schema change. EN + PL. Zielone: `tsc`/**454 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Search/filter in long admin lists (audit v3 UX)** **(#620)** ‚ÄĒ admins with many achievements or shop items had to eyeball a long scroll; now a **search box** appears above the **Achievements** and **Shop** lists (shown once a list passes 8 items) and filters them live. New pure **`lib/list-filter`** ‚ÄĒ **diacritic-insensitive** (typing `zolw`/`lodz` finds `ŇĽ√≥Ňāw`/`ŇĀ√≥dŇļ`; folds Polish accents incl. `Ňā‚Üíl`) and **token-AND** (each typed word narrows further) ‚ÄĒ plus a reusable presentational **`ListSearch`** primitive (search icon + clear button + a `shown/total` count) in `admin/shared`, ready for any other list to adopt. Achievements filters by name/code/rarity/trigger/reward-note; Shop by name/category/sub-tier. Client-only, no API/schema change. **+10 tests ‚Üí 449.** EN + PL (shared `common.searchPlaceholder`/`noResults`). Zielone: `tsc`/**449 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **GDPR data export ‚ÄĒ "download my data" (audit v3)** **(#619)** ‚ÄĒ completes the privacy story we built (encrypted PII #609, erasure, policy #610): a viewer can now **download everything we store about their account** as a JSON file from `/profile` ‚ÄĒ the GDPR **right of access (Art. 15) + portability (Art. 20)** companion to the existing one-click erasure. New **`GET /api/profile/export`** (owner-only, strictly scoped to `session.user.id`, rate-limited 5/5min) gathers the account, economy, progression, social links, GT ledger (capped at 5 000, flagged if trimmed), achievements, collectibles, followed portals, companion, and shipping PII (**decrypted for the owner only**), and streams it as a `Content-Disposition: attachment` file. **Secret material is never exported** ‚ÄĒ the pure `lib/data-export` shaper redacts the TOTP secret, passkey keys and OAuth tokens, emitting only presence (`totpEnabled`, `passkeys: N`); internal moderation notes and other people's data are excluded by design. A small self-contained `DataExportCard` on `/profile` (fetch ‚Üí client-side download). Pure `lib/data-export` (`buildUserExport` redaction + `exportFilename` slug, **+8 tests ‚Üí 439**). No schema change. EN + PL. Zielone: `tsc`/**439 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Per-portal game library (audit v3, white-label)** **(#618)** ‚ÄĒ the game library (`/games`, synced from Steam/PSN) was the **last globally-keyed feature**: `Game` had a global `@@unique([source, externalId])`, so two portals couldn't each own the same Steam appid and every portal saw the founder's library. Now `Game` gains a nullable **`tenantId`** and the unique becomes the per-tenant composite **`@@unique([tenantId, source, externalId])`** (+`@@index([tenantId])`) ‚ÄĒ **db push** (the unique swap needs `--accept-data-loss`; no real loss ‚ÄĒ the column is all-NULL and rows stay unique under the new key). The Steam/PSN sync now writes `tenantId` (from the per-tenant `GameLibraryConfig`), **bulk-claims any legacy NULL-tenant rows for the portal before upserting** (so a re-sync updates them in place instead of creating duplicates ‚ÄĒ robust regardless of backfill order), prunes only the portal's own rows, and uses a NULL-safe upsert helper (Prisma can't key an upsert on a compound unique with a NULL member). All reads are scoped **OR-null** (`/api/games`, `/games`, `/admin#games` count/aggregate/list) and `toggle_hidden` is tenant-guarded (`updateMany` by id+tenant ‚Üí can't flip another portal's game). Existing rows are attached to the founder by **`/api/admin/backfill-tenant`** (now also backfills `Game`). **Per-tenant PSN/Xbox *connect* (sensitive NPSSO per portal) remains a subdomain-milestone follow-up** ‚ÄĒ the NPSSO is still a single global env. Founder portal unchanged (its rows claim/backfill to its tenant). Zielone: `tsc`/**431 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Support-engagement alerts, streamer-selectable channel (audit v3)** **(#614)** ‚ÄĒ the streamer can now be alerted when a viewer opens/copies a tip method on `/support`. New `Tenant.supportAlertMode` (**db push** ‚ÄĒ additive, default `"none"`), chosen in `/admin#tenants`: **`bell`** (in-app notification to the portal owner), **`overlay`** (an OBS alert the overlay renders by icon, created directly ‚ÄĒ no `enabledTypes` gate, like sound redemptions), **`both`**, or **`none`**. Hooked into the existing `/api/support/click` beacon, **throttled to one alert per method per 5 min** (a click is an intent signal, not a confirmed payment ‚ÄĒ fail-closed so a limiter blip can't spam) and fully best-effort (never blocks the beacon). Honestly framed in the alert copy ("possible support"). No new alert-type plumbing. Zielone: `tsc`/**431 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Per-portal social links (white-label, audit v3)** **(#613)** ‚ÄĒ the streamer's social icons in the footer / about / welcome were **hard-coded to the founder's channels**, so every white-label portal showed Gh0s77tt's socials. Now each portal sets **its own** links: new `Tenant.socialLinks` JSON (**db push** ‚ÄĒ additive nullable column, applied) edited in `/admin#tenants` (one `platform url` per line; platforms: discord/twitch/kick/youtube/tiktok/instagram/x ‚ÄĒ server-validated against that set + `safeMediaUrl`). `SocialLinksRow`/`SocialLinksGrid` take an optional `links` prop and reuse the existing brand icons/colours by platform; threaded from the footer, `/about` and `/welcome`. **Falls back to the founder default (`SOCIALS`) when unset**, so the founder portal is byte-for-byte unchanged (verified: footer still renders the 7 default icons). Defensive parse on read. EN + PL admin labels. Zielone: `tsc`/**431 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Chat-keyword raffle with sub/mod odds (audit v3)** **(#611)** ‚ÄĒ the classic "type a word in chat to enter, streamer draws later" giveaway. A raffle (`/admin#events`) can now carry an optional **chat keyword** (free entry, alongside the existing paid tickets) plus **per-sub / per-mod ticket weights** (default 2√ó each) so subs & mods get **higher odds**. New `Event.raffleKeyword` + `raffleSubWeight`/`raffleModWeight` (**db push** ‚ÄĒ additive, applied). The bot reports a keyword hit to the new **`POST /api/internal/raffle-entry`** (Bearer `BOT_SECRET`): it finds the active keyword raffle for the portal, resolves the chat user to a **linked** account (tenant-scoped), and grants `weight` tickets ‚ÄĒ **one entry per user** (repeat hits ignored). The existing crypto-secure draw already weights by ticket count, so no draw change. **‚ö†ÔłŹ Bot coordination required:** the `ghost-empire-chat` bot must call the new endpoint on each keyword match (payload `{ keyword, platform, username, isSub, isMod }`) ‚ÄĒ until then the admin config is dormant. Admin create + edit forms gained the 3 fields. EN + PL. Zielone: `tsc`/**426 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Encrypted shipping/contact profile for physical rewards (audit v3)** **(#609)** ‚ÄĒ viewers can now store the shipping details needed to send them a **physical prize** (full name, phone, email, address, city, postal code, country, **parcel locker** e.g. InPost). New **`ShippingProfile`** model (**db push** ‚ÄĒ new table, applied) kept deliberately **out of the heavily-`select`ed `users` table** so it can never be swept into a select-less query and can be dropped independently. **Every sensitive field is encrypted at rest** (AES-256-GCM via `lib/crypto`, `enc:v1:` envelope); only `country` (ISO-2) is plaintext. `GET/PUT/DELETE /api/profile/shipping` is strictly scoped to `session.user.id` (owner-only, rate-limited): **PUT requires an explicit consent checkbox** (GDPR Art. 6/7, stamps `consentAt`) and re-encrypts; **DELETE is one-click GDPR erasure**. A self-contained, collapsible **`ShippingProfileCard`** on `/profile` (loads on open, privacy note, consent, save/delete) ‚ÄĒ never exposed publicly. Pure `lib/shipping` (`cleanShippingInput`/`hasAnyShipping`, **+8 tests ‚Üí 426**). EN + PL. **Note:** for production, set a dedicated `ENCRYPTION_KEY` (else the key derives from `NEXTAUTH_SECRET`); admin-side fulfillment view is a follow-up. Zielone: `tsc`/**426 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Per-portal background image (audit v3)** **(#608)** ‚ÄĒ streamers can set a custom **background image** for their whole portal (`/admin#tenants` ‚Üí "Background image URL"). New `Tenant.bgImageUrl` (**db push** ‚ÄĒ additive nullable column, applied), rendered **as the `<body>` background behind a strong dark gradient overlay** (`rgba(0,0,0,.86‚Üí.93)`) so text contrast/readability is fully preserved; `background-attachment: fixed` for a subtle parallax. The URL is sanitized with `safeMediaUrl` **both on write and on read** (it lands in a CSS `url()`, so double-guarded against injection / `javascript:`/`data:`). Null = the current look, unchanged (verified: no `background-image` emitted when unset). EN + PL label. Zielone: `tsc`/**418 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Per-portal default companion name (audit v3)** **(#607)** ‚ÄĒ streamers can now name the Ghost Companion for their whole portal instead of every viewer's pet defaulting to the hard-coded "Widmo". New `Tenant.companionDefaultName` (**db push** ‚ÄĒ additive nullable column, applied) editable in `/admin#tenants`; a freshly-created companion (`GET /api/companion` create-on-read) starts with the portal's name (resolved via the React-cached `getCurrentTenant`, so **no extra query**), falling back to "Widmo" when unset. Viewers can still rename their own companion. EN + PL label. Zielone: `tsc`/**418 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Semantic search (dormant)** **(#554)** ‚ÄĒ direction 3: a `/search` page that ranks the portal's content by **meaning, not keywords** ‚ÄĒ describe what you want ("how do I support the streamer?") and it returns the closest pages, achievements and shop items. Uses **AI embeddings** (`aiEmbed` ‚Üí OpenAI `text-embedding-3-small`) + cosine similarity; **dormant until an OpenAI key is set** (clear "not switched on" note, with the Ctrl/‚Ćė K palette as the fallback). Corpus = static pages + per-tenant achievements/shop; **corpus + query embeddings cached in-memory** per instance (one batch embed on a cold start, nothing re-embedded while warm). Pure `lib/semantic` (`cosineSim`/`rankBySimilarity`, **+4 tests**); per-IP rate-limited. In the Ctrl/‚Ćė K palette. No schema change. EN + PL. Zielone: `tsc`/**387 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **P2P GT gifting** **(#553)** ‚ÄĒ direction 2: viewers can **send %gt% to each other**. A "Send %gt%" button on a viewer's public profile (`/u/<name>`, for logged-in non-owners) ‚Üí amount ‚Üí `POST /api/gift`. The debit + credit + both ledger rows are **one atomic transaction** (`gte` guard ‚Üí no overspend); anti-abuse: **can't gift yourself**, **5 000 per-transfer + 10 000 rolling-24h caps**, per-IP rate-limited, recipient resolved **within the same portal**. The recipient gets a best-effort in-app **notification** (created outside the tx so it can never undo a real transfer). No new model (existing `Transaction`/`Notification`). Pure `lib/gift` (`clampGift`/`giftError`, **+5 tests**). EN + PL. Zielone: `tsc`/**383 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **P2P card marketplace** **(#552)** ‚ÄĒ marketplace phase 2: viewers **trade collectible cards (#551) for %gt%** on `/market`. List a card you own (it's **escrowed** ‚ÄĒ removed from your collection while listed), browse others' listings and **buy**, or cancel to get the card back. Every GT + card move is **one atomic transaction** with `gte`/`qty` guards: the listing is claimed with a conditional `UPDATE` (so two concurrent buys yield exactly one sale), overspend is impossible, you can't buy your own listing, and a failed payment rolls the whole thing back. A **5% fee is burned** on each sale (a GT sink, reviewed for value-conservation). Model `CardListing` (**db push** ‚ÄĒ new table, per-tenant). Pure `lib/market` (price clamp + fee, **+3 tests**); buy/sell/my-listings UI. In the Community nav + Ctrl/‚Ćė K. EN + PL. Zielone: `tsc`/**378 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Collectible cards + GT packs** **(#551)** ‚ÄĒ marketplace phase 1: the **tradeable asset** the P2P market (#552) will sit on. A per-portal card catalog (`/admin#collectibles` ‚ÄĒ name, **rarity**, emoji/image) that viewers collect on `/collectibles` by **opening GT packs** ‚ÄĒ one card per pack, **weighted by rarity** (common 60 / rare 28 / epic 10 / legendary 2). The GT spend + ownership grant + ledger entry are **one atomic transaction** (`tokens: { gte }` guard ‚Üí overspend-proof). Models `Collectible` + `UserCollectible` (**db push** ‚ÄĒ new tables, per-tenant). Pure `lib/collectibles` (`pickRarity`/weights, **+5 tests**). Collection grid shows owned cards in full colour (√óqty) and the rest as dimmed silhouettes. In the Community nav + Ctrl/‚Ćė K. EN + PL. Zielone: `tsc`/**375 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Visual overlay scene builder** **(#550)** ‚ÄĒ the marquee OBS feature: compose **several overlay widgets on one 16:9 canvas** (`/admin#scenes`) ‚ÄĒ drag to move, drag the corner to resize, delete ‚ÄĒ then drop a **single browser source** `/overlay/scene/<id>?token=‚Ä¶` into OBS for the whole scene. The render **composites the existing overlays as transparent positioned iframes**, so none of the ~19 overlay pages had to change. Per-tenant scenes (model `OverlayScene`, **db push** ‚ÄĒ new table; elements stored as validated JSON). - **AI chat translation on the OBS overlay (dormant)** **(#547)** ‚ÄĒ append **`?translate=<lang>`** (e.g. `pl`, `en`, `de`) to the chat browser-source URL and foreign messages get an **AI translation shown muted under each line** ‚ÄĒ so a streamer can read an international chat live. Off the chat-ingest hot path (translation happens in the overlay render, per-message, **client- and server-cached** so the 2s feed refresh never re-translates, and gated by a pure `shouldTranslate` that skips emotes/links/commands/short text). `POST /api/chat/translate` (per-IP rate-limited, `cacheJson`-cached) reuses the shared `aiChat` ‚ÄĒ **dormant until an AI key is set** (`/admin#integrations`), exactly like Recap/Clip Director. - **Profile accent colour** **(#546)** ‚ÄĒ a viewer can tint **their own public profile** (`/u/<name>`) with one of 10 accent presets ‚ÄĒ it recolours the **avatar ring + name glow**, complementing the country flag (#540). - **Passkeys ‚ÄĒ passwordless sign-in (stage 2)** **(#544)** ‚ÄĒ a **"Sign in with a passkey"** button on the sign-in page completes the feature: a usernameless/discoverable WebAuthn assertion is verified server-side, and on success a **session is minted directly** ‚ÄĒ a `Session` row + the host-only `authjs.session-token` cookie, an **exact replication of NextAuth's database-session sign-in** (cookie name/attrs/value verified against `@auth/core`). **It never reads or alters the NextAuth config or the OAuth providers** ‚ÄĒ it only ADDS a session for that browser, so the worst possible failure is "didn't sign in," never "broke OAuth login." Routes `/api/auth/passkey/login/{options,verify}`; the signature counter advances on each use (clone detection). No schema change. **Needs a real-device test on the live site** (WebAuthn needs HTTPS + an authenticator ‚ÄĒ can't be exercised locally). EN + PL. Zielone: `tsc`/**341 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Passkeys ‚ÄĒ registration & management (stage 1)** **(#543)** ‚ÄĒ viewers can add **passkeys** (fingerprint / face / device PIN) to their account from a self-hiding "Passkeys" card on `/profile`: a full WebAuthn registration ceremony (`/api/auth/passkey/register/options` ‚Üí `‚Ä¶/verify`, challenge stashed in a short-lived httpOnly cookie) backed by `@simplewebauthn/server`, plus list/remove (`/api/auth/passkey`). **Deliberately additive and isolated ‚ÄĒ touches ZERO of the existing OAuth login flow**; the model `Passkey` (per-user, `credentialId @unique`, **db push** ‚ÄĒ new table) just stores credentials. Pure `lib/webauthn` host/origin helpers (**+5 tests**). New deps `@simplewebauthn/server`+`browser`. **Signing IN with a passkey is the next stage (#544)** ‚ÄĒ it'll mint a `Session` row directly (DB-session strategy), still without altering the NextAuth config. EN + PL. Zielone: `tsc`/**341 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.

Additive model `PortalFollow` (**db push**), pure `lib/portal-hub` (`portalUrl`/`buildPortalList`, +8 tests) ‚ÄĒ switch URLs light up once subdomains deploy (`NEXT_PUBLIC_ROOT_DOMAIN`). - **Portal-wide help assistant on every page** **(#507)** ‚ÄĒ a floating "?" mounted in the locale layout: always-on **static help** (quick links + 5-item FAQ) for everyone, plus an **AI chat** for logged-in viewers that degrades gracefully (reuses `aiChat`; no AI plan/key ‚Üí a clean "unavailable" note, static help carries it). Per-user rate-limited; hidden on `/admin` (its own assistant), absent on OBS overlays. EN + PL, other locales fall back to EN. No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**283 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.

### Fixed

- **next-intl `INVALID_KEY` noise from dotted message keys** **(#597)** ‚ÄĒ every page render logged ~30√ó `INVALID_KEY: Namespace keys cannot contain the character "."` (thrown from `getTranslations` in the locale layout + `page` `generateMetadata`) because eight Twitch/Kick event-type labels were keyed by their **literal dotted event names** (`admin.twitchEventSub.eventType."channel.subscribe"`, `admin.kickEvents.eventLabel."livestream.status.updated"`, ‚Ä¶), which next-intl reads as nesting separators ‚ÄĒ so those keys never resolved (silent EN fallback) and the log was pure noise. Renamed all eight to a safe **underscore** separator (`channel_subscribe`, `livestream_status_updated`, ‚Ä¶) across **all 14 locale catalogs** (key parity intact, EN stays the deep-merge base), matching the existing underscore convention already used in `webhooksOut.eventLabel`; the two consumers (`TwitchEventSub`/`KickEvents`) now normalize the dotted raw event type (`type.replace(/\./g, "_")`) before the `t.raw(...)` label lookup, so labels still render. Data + 2 components only, no schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**412 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.

### Security

- **Verified-only donation crediting via a personal code (audit v3)** **(#612)** ‚ÄĒ closes the within-tenant half of the Streamlabs spoofing finding (#601 fixed cross-tenant). The old auto-match credited GT by the **donor-supplied name / `@mention`**, so a payer could aim a donation's GT at **any account**. Removed entirely: `matchDonationToUser` now auto-credits **only** when the donation message contains the donor's **personal code** (`GE-XXXXXX`, shown on their profile, lazily minted, globally unique) ‚ÄĒ resolved tenant-scoped; everything else falls to the **manual admin queue** (`/api/admin/donations`, unchanged). New `User.donationCode` (**db push** ‚ÄĒ additive nullable unique column, applied with `--accept-data-loss` for the new-column unique, owner-approved; no real data loss ‚ÄĒ all rows null). New `GET /api/profile/donation-code` (owner-only, lazy-mint w/ collision retry) + a **`DonationCodeCard`** on `/profile` (code + copy + how-to). Pure `lib/donation-code` (`generate`/`extract`/`isValid`, **+5 tests ‚Üí 431**). EN + PL. Zielone: `tsc`/**431 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Security hardening sweep ‚ÄĒ TOTP / passkey / webhook / CSRF + donation GT cap (audit v3)** **(#602)** ‚ÄĒ five low/medium findings from the v3 audit, all no-schema: (1) **TOTP step-up** compared the 6-digit code with `===` ‚Üí now a **constant-time** `timingSafeEqual` so a near-miss can't be probed digit-by-digit (RFC test vectors still green). (2) **Passkey login** wrote back the signature counter but never rejected a **non-advancing counter** (the classic cloned-authenticator signal) ‚Üí now refuses the login when `newCounter !== 0 && newCounter <= stored`. (3) **Outbound webhooks** ran the SSRF guard on the original URL but `fetch` followed redirects ‚Üí added **`redirect:"manual"`** so an admin-set public URL can't 302 into `169.254.169.254`/internal (a 3xx is counted as a failure). (4) **Streamlabs OAuth callback** skipped the CSRF-nonce check when the cookie was absent ‚Üí now **requires** the cookie AND a match. (5) **Streamlabs donation GT** minted `amount √ó GT_PER_PLN` **ignoring currency** and uncapped ‚Üí now **currency-converted** via `plnFromCurrency` and **capped** at ~100k-PLN-equivalent so a non-PLN or malformed-huge upstream amount can't over-mint. No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**418 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Scope donation / sub / cheer crediting to the event's portal (audit v3)** **(#601)** ‚ÄĒ a fresh deep audit found the GT-crediting lookups for **Streamlabs donations** and **Twitch/Kick sub¬∑gift¬∑cheer** events resolved the credited user by **username globally, with no tenant filter** ‚ÄĒ so a real (signed/verified) event on portal A whose donor-name/Twitch-login also exists on portal B would **mint GT into portal B's economy** (a cross-tenant economic leak; also the donor-supplied name/`@mention` in Streamlabs let a payer aim the credit at any same-named account). All six webhook credit lookups (`twitch-eventsub` sub/gift/cheer, `kick-events` sub/gift/cheer) now scope the `Connection` match by **`user.tenantId`**, and `matchDonationToUser` (Streamlabs) scopes by **`User.tenantId`** threaded from the connection ‚ÄĒ both using the established **`OR: [{tenantId}, {tenantId: null}]`** back-compat pattern, so single-tenant (null tenant) behaviour is byte-for-byte unchanged and only multi-tenant crediting gets isolated. No schema change, no db push. (Deferred to a follow-up: the within-tenant donor-name spoofing hardening ‚ÄĒ needs an owner call on disabling name/mention auto-match ‚ÄĒ plus Streamlabs currency-aware GT cap and the LOW hardenings: TOTP constant-time compare, passkey clone-counter rejection, outbound-webhook `redirect:"manual"`.) Zielone: `tsc`/**418 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Cross-tenant scoping for stream/donation/moderation data + per-tenant bot secret (Batch B, audit v2)** **(#599)** ‚ÄĒ the last audit-v2 gap: four bot/webhook-fed models had **no `tenantId`**, so their data was a single global pool ‚ÄĒ latent at single-tenant, but a cross-tenant leak the moment subdomains light up. Added a **nullable `tenantId`** (+ index) to **`StreamSession`**, **`Donation`** and **`ModViolationLog`** and a nullable **`Tenant.botSecret`** (**db push** ‚ÄĒ all additive, no `--accept-data-loss`). Writes now tag the resolved portal: stream-session create/close carry the EventSub-resolved tenant (and one portal's `stream.offline` can no longer close another's live session), Streamlabs/YouTube donations use the connection's `tenantId`, mod-violation logs use `currentTenantId()`. Admin reads scope to the caller's tenant (`/api/admin/analytics` sessions, `/api/admin/mod-violations` stats, `/api/admin/section-data` unmatched donations) and the manual donation-match (`/api/admin/donations`) refuses another portal's donation. New **`verifyBotSecretForTenant`** (+6 tests) accepts a tenant's own `botSecret` **or** the global `BOT_SECRET` as fallback. **Fully backward-compatible / latent**: at single-tenant `currentTenantId()` is null ‚Üí writes tag null, reads stay unscoped ‚Üí identical behaviour; the global bot secret keeps working. **Deferred within this batch:** scoping the `ChatActivityBucket` heatmap (needs a destructive composite-PK change ‚ÄĒ done at subdomain-enable) and *enforcing* per-tenant bot secrets (needs each tenant running its own bot, coordinated with the `ghost-empire-chat` repo). Zielone: `tsc`/**418 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Atomic gift daily-cap + account-XP under concurrency (audit v2)** **(#573)** ‚ÄĒ two read-modify-write races, both fixed with a `SELECT ‚Ä¶ FOR UPDATE` row lock on the affected user: (1) **Gift daily cap** ‚ÄĒ the rolling-24h `GIFT_DAILY_LIMIT` was checked *before* the transfer transaction, so a burst of concurrent gifts each passed the stale pre-check and committed, **defeating the anti-laundering cap** (balance was still safe via the `gte` guard); the cap is now **re-asserted inside the locked transaction**. (2) **Account XP** ‚ÄĒ `awardAccountXp` read `xp`, added, then wrote the **absolute** value, so concurrent awards on the hot chat-award path clobbered each other (ended at `X+max(a,b)`, not `X+a+b`); now the read‚Üícompute‚Üíwrite runs under the row lock (level/prestige/bonus derived from the locked value), with the alert + achievement side-effects moved **after commit**. No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**401 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Scope admin reads to the resolved tenant (audit v2)** **(#572)** ‚ÄĒ four admin reads ignored the host tenant and hit a global/legacy row, leaking or mis-showing another portal's data: **`/api/admin/alerts`** listed recent alerts with **no `where`** (exposed other tenants' alert actor names + donation/sub amounts) ‚Üí now scoped to `{ tenantId }` (+ legacy null); **`/api/admin/section-data?s=bot`** read/created the legacy `id:"default"` `BotConfig` ‚Üí now the tenant's row (mirrors `admin/bot-config`), so a tenant admin no longer sees/edits the founder's reward rates; **`/api/admin/stream-goals`** read the `id:"default"` `HypeTrainState` ‚Üí now per-tenant (mirrors overlay-feeds); **`/api/admin/setup-status`** read `moderationConfig.findFirst()` (an arbitrary portal's row) ‚Üí now scoped. All three models already have `tenantId @unique`; only these reads were unscoped. No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**401 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Rate-limit the un-capped cost/abuse endpoints (audit v2)** **(#571)** ‚ÄĒ three endpoints could run up cost or fan-out unbounded: **`POST /api/admin/recap`** made a real LLM call (+ optional Discord post) with **no limiter** (every other AI route self-limits) ‚Üí now **10/5min per admin**; **`POST /api/push/test`** fanned out to the user's devices + the external push provider on every call ‚Üí now **5/min per user**; **`POST /api/bot/ai-reply`** was limited only by the **attacker-controllable** `username` key ‚Üí added a **global cap (300/h)** so rotating usernames can't multiply AI spend (mirrors `bot/imagine`). No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**401 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Resolver atomicity + admin step-up (audit v2)** **(#569)** ‚ÄĒ four correctness/authz gaps from the second audit: (1) **Heist double-resolve** ‚ÄĒ `resolveHeist` did a plain read + unconditional `update`, so the bot timer racing the lazy recovery-on-join could both run the payout loop and **double-credit the crew**; now it **atomically claims** the heist (`updateMany open‚Üíresolving`, bail on `count===0`) like predictions/duels. (2) **weekly-rewards cron paid a single GLOBAL top-3** (`getCachedWeeklyRanking(null)`) while the ranking pages are per-tenant, and its idempotency was a global check-then-act; now it **loops every portal**, pays each its own top-3, and guards with a **per-tenant-per-week unique `externalId`** (a double cron-fire loses with P2002, atomically). (3) **Role grants lacked step-up** ‚ÄĒ `admin`/`moderator` changes (the most powerful, role-conferring actions) were weaker than a reversible `ban-user`; now they **require a fresh 2FA code** (`requireStepUp`, no-op without 2FA; client uses `apiPostStepUp`). (4) **Admin token deduction** wasn't atomic (stale pre-check + unguarded `increment`); now a `gte`-guarded `updateMany` so concurrent deducts can't drive a balance negative. No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**401 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Casino concurrency hardening ‚ÄĒ per-session lock on stateful games (audit v2)** **(#568)** ‚ÄĒ a second deep audit found the stateful Redis games did **non-atomic read-modify-write** with no lock: in Mines `reveal` / Hi-Lo `guess`, two concurrent moves could interleave so a winning-tile `set` lands *after* a losing-tile `del`, **resurrecting a session that should have ended** (erasing the loss ‚Üí GT over-payout); Blackjack `double` also charged a second bet *before* claiming the session (concurrent doubles ‚Üí an extra debit with no game). New **`withLock`** in `lib/redis` (Redis `SET NX PX` + atomic Lua compare-and-delete release, auto-expiring) now serializes every in-place session mutation ‚ÄĒ Mines `reveal`, Hi-Lo `guess`, Blackjack `hit`/`stand`/`double` ‚ÄĒ so concurrent moves on one session can't interleave (the loser gets a 409 "retry"). Cash-out/settle were already atomic via `GETDEL`; this closes the intermediate race. Fail-open if Redis blips (the `GETDEL` claims still protect payouts). No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**401 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Clear all `npm audit` alerts via overrides (no breaking downgrades)** **(#567)** ‚ÄĒ the 5 moderate advisories were all **transitive dev/build** deps: `postcss <8.5.10` (CSS-stringify XSS, GHSA-qx2v-qp2m-jg93) pinned by **`next`**, and `@hono/node-server <1.19.13` (serveStatic middleware bypass, GHSA-92pp-h63x-v22m) pulled by **`@prisma/dev`** (Prisma 7 tooling). `npm audit fix --force` wanted to downgrade `next`‚Üí9 / `prisma`‚Üí6 ‚ÄĒ rejected. Instead added npm **`overrides`**: `postcss ^8.5.10` scoped under `next` (so it dedupes to the already-installed 8.5.15) and `@hono/node-server ^1.19.13`. Lockfile regenerated to apply them; **verified no runtime dep changed** (next/react/prisma/next-auth/next-intl/stripe/zod all identical) and the **Vercel Linux native binaries** (`@next/swc-linux-*`, `lightningcss-linux-x64-gnu`, `@tailwindcss/oxide-linux-x64-gnu`, `@img/sharp-linux-x64`) are intact. **`npm audit` now: 0 vulnerabilities.** No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**401 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build` + `npm audit` clean.
- **Audit follow-up ‚ÄĒ medium-severity fixes (M1/M2/M3/M4)** **(#556)** ‚ÄĒ second pass from the same audit, all multi-tenant / concurrency correctness:
  - **M1 ‚ÄĒ overlay token cross-tenant leak:** `isValidOverlayToken` (`lib/alerts`) accepted the legacy "default" row's token AND the global `OVERLAY_TOKEN` env var for **any** tenant ‚ÄĒ so one portal's (or the env) token could drive another portal's OBS overlay. Now **strict 1:1**: a real tenant validates only against its own `overlayToken`; the default-row + env fallback survive only for the legacy/founder portal (`tid === null`, the owner's own).
  - **M2 ‚ÄĒ merge-users null-tenant bypass:** the tenant-isolation guard only ran `if (tid)` and used `u.tenantId && u.tenantId !== tid`, so a per-tenant admin could merge (and thereby delete) a **null-tenant** (legacy/global) user. Now strict equality (`u.tenantId !== tid`), **always enforced** for non-platform-owners ‚ÄĒ both users must belong to exactly the acting admin's portal.
  - **M3 ‚ÄĒ predictions TOCTOU:** `resolvePrediction` snapshotted entries + pot, then claimed the row ‚ÄĒ a wager committing in between left a paid-for stake unpaid. Wager / resolve / cancel now take a **`SELECT ‚Ä¶ FOR UPDATE`** row lock on the prediction up front, serializing all three on that row.
  - **M4 ‚ÄĒ daily-bonus double-claim:** replaced the Serializable-isolation + in-tx re-check with a **deterministic unique `externalId`** (`daily-bonus:<userId>:<utcDay>`) on the already-unique `Transaction.externalId` ‚ÄĒ two concurrent claims race on the unique index and exactly one wins (P2002). (The drops "first-N bonus" atomic counter, also M4, rides the batched perf-index **db push** in a later PR.)
  No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**392 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Security hardening from a full audit (C1/H1/H2/H3)** **(#555)** ‚ÄĒ fixes four access-control / SSRF gaps found in an adversarial pass over the admin + outbound-fetch surface:
  - **C1 ‚ÄĒ destructive admin reset was per-tenant-admin reachable:** `POST /api/admin/reset-database` runs **global** `deleteMany`s that span EVERY tenant, but was gated by `requireAdmin` (any portal admin). Now gated by **`requirePlatformOwner`** + a **fresh-2FA step-up** (`requireStepUp` ‚ÄĒ the single most destructive action in the app), with the danger-zone UI retrying via `apiPostStepUp`.
  - **H1 ‚ÄĒ cross-tenant data export:** `GET /api/admin/backup` reads every user's GT balance + role flags across **all** tenants (empty `where`), also only `requireAdmin`. Now **`requirePlatformOwner`**.
  - **H2 ‚ÄĒ unauthenticated IDOR on link analytics:** `POST /api/profile/social-click` did `update({ where: { id } })` from a raw client id ‚ÄĒ any id could bump (or cross-tenant forge) another user's click counter. Now an **`updateMany` scoped to a link whose owner is in the current portal** (mirrors the support/click route).
  - **H3 ‚ÄĒ SSRF via admin webhooks:** outgoing webhooks (`lib/webhooks-out`) `fetch`ed admin-set URLs with no destination check. New **`lib/ssrf-guard`** (`isSafeWebhookUrl` ‚ÄĒ rejects loopback/private/link-local/CGNAT/cloud-metadata both as IP literals AND after DNS resolution; `http(s)` only) is now enforced before every delivery and surfaced on the test button (**+ unit tests**).
  - Also unblocks the type gate: `scripts/seed-collectibles.ts` was a global script colliding with `seed-achievements.ts` on top-level `main` (TS2393) ‚ÄĒ marked it a module with `export {};` (the `backfill-account-tenant.ts` pattern). This was making a fresh `tsc` (CI) red.
  No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**392 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Hardening pass from an adversarial review of the new auth + push code** **(#545)** ‚ÄĒ two self-reviews of the just-shipped passkey (#543/#544) and web-push (#533‚Äď#535) code surfaced fixable gaps (no auth-bypass; the core crypto + tenant isolation were already correct):
  - **Passkeys:** `rpID`/`origin` **and** the minted session cookie's name/`secure` are now pinned to the canonical `AUTH_URL`/`NEXTAUTH_URL` instead of the spoofable `Host`/`X-Forwarded-Proto` headers (kills host-header trust + guarantees the cookie matches what NextAuth reads); the WebAuthn **challenge is strictly single-use** (cookie cleared on every terminal path, not just success); login now **requires user verification** (biometric/PIN ‚ÄĒ appropriate for a sole login factor); the login endpoints are **rate-limited** and no longer leak a **credential-existence oracle** (generic `not-verified` for unknown-vs-failed); client-supplied `transports` are whitelisted. (+4 tests.)
  - **Web push:** the "LIVE now" push is now **fire-and-forget** in the Twitch EventSub webhook (was `await`ed ‚ÄĒ a slow push endpoint could have stalled the webhook ‚Üí Twitch retries / DB-pool exhaustion), and every `web-push` send now carries a **5s timeout** so a black-holed endpoint can't hang the function; defensive `.catch` on all fire-and-forget `notify*` call sites.
  No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**345 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.

### Performance

- **Aggregate poll/prediction tallies in the DB instead of loading every row (audit v3)** **(#606)** ‚ÄĒ two read-hot paths pulled whole child tables to count in JS. **`POST /api/polls/vote`** re-read **every `PollVote` row** of the poll on each vote (`findMany` + `.filter().length` per option) ‚Üí now one **`groupBy`** (the table already has `@@index([pollId, optionIndex])`), matching the pattern the overlay feed already uses. **`GET /api/predictions`** (public, `force-dynamic`) loaded **all `PredictionEntry` rows of every open prediction** on each request to compute per-option totals ‚Üí now a single **`groupBy(["predictionId","optionIndex"])`** across all active predictions plus **one scoped `findMany`** for the caller's own entries (`myEntry`). A hyped poll/prediction with thousands of entries no longer streams them all per request ‚ÄĒ big win on the 3-connection pool. (P3 ‚ÄĒ batching the per-loser `notification.create` in prediction resolve/cancel ‚ÄĒ left as low-value/money-path-adjacent.) No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**418 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Atomic + batched stream-goal increments; batched daily-quest progress (audit v2)** **(#600)** ‚ÄĒ a fresh-eyes pass on the event hot paths found two per-row write loops. **`incrementGoals`** (fires on every sub / gift-sub / follow / donation / cheer / YT-member) read each active goal, computed `current + amount` in JS, then wrote the **absolute** value back per goal in a loop ‚ÄĒ a **read-modify-write lost-update race** (two concurrent monetary events both read `current`, both wrote the sum ‚Üí one bump silently lost, goal bars undercount), the same class as the account-XP fix (#573), plus an N-query loop. Now it's **one atomic `updateMany({ current: { increment } })`** for all matching goals (no lost updates under concurrency) + a single guarded `updateMany` to stamp `completedAt` on goals that crossed their target ‚ÄĒ **2 queries, race-free**, in a `$transaction`. **`updateDailyTaskProgress`** (fires on every awarded chat/Discord message) issued **N sequential `upsert`s** (one per active quest of that type) on the 3-connection pool ‚Üí now one **`$transaction`** of the same upserts (one round-trip; each upsert keeps its atomic create-or-increment, so semantics are unchanged). No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**418 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Perf tail ‚ÄĒ OG cache + parallel entry reads (audit v2)** **(#576)** ‚ÄĒ the profile **OG image** (`/u/<name>` opengraph-image) had no `revalidate`, so every social-scrape re-ran a Prisma read + Satori PNG render ‚Üí added `revalidate = 600` (10 min). `/api/clips` and `/api/collectibles` awaited `auth()` then `currentTenantId()` **serially** ‚Üí now `Promise.all([...])` so the two independent reads don't stack a round-trip on the 3-connection pool. No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**401 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Cache the public `/support` page + casino leaderboard (audit v2)** **(#575)** ‚ÄĒ both were fully uncached public reads. `/support` ran **5 DB queries** (incl. a `groupBy` for top supporters) **plus CPU-bound per-method QR generation** on every visit ‚Üí the whole shaped blob is now `cacheJson`-cached per tenant (**60s**), and the page-QR per host (**5min**). `GET /api/gt-games/leaderboard` ran a **30-day `groupBy`** over the high-volume casino table per request ‚Üí now cached per tenant (**60s**, mirrors `getCachedRanking`). Big drop in DB/CPU work on two hot public paths (3-connection pool). No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**401 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Chat-award hot path ‚ÄĒ ack-first, secondary effects in background (audit v2)** **(#574)** ‚ÄĒ `/api/internal/chat-award` fires **once per chat message across Twitch/Kick/YouTube** (the single hottest write path) and ran, strictly serially after the GT award, three more best-effort effects ‚ÄĒ battle-pass XP (`awardSeasonXp`), daily-quest progress (`updateDailyTaskProgress`) and the activity-heatmap upsert ‚ÄĒ ~6 extra serial round-trips on a **3-connection** pool. The bot only needs `awarded`/`newBalance`, so those three now run in **`after()`** (post-response, `waitUntil`); the bot's per-message call returns right after the award transaction. No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**401 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Timeouts on all third-party API calls (audit v2)** **(#570)** ‚ÄĒ outbound calls to **Twitch / Kick / YouTube / Streamlabs / Steam** had **no timeout**, so a slow/black-holed upstream could hang a serverless function and **pin one of the 3 DB-pool slots** indefinitely (e.g. `helixGet` backs the live-status banner; Kick `getPublicKey` is on the webhook signature-verification path). New **`lib/http.httpFetch`** wraps `fetch` with a default **8s `AbortSignal.timeout`** (override via your own `signal`); every external `fetch` in those five clients now goes through it, so a stuck upstream **fails fast** instead of hanging (callers already handle the rejection). No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**401 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Per-tenant composite indexes + atomic drop-bonus counter** **(#561)** ‚ÄĒ one batched **db push** (additive, no data loss). Six composite indexes for hot tenant-scoped reads that the existing single-column indexes didn't cover: `Companion[tenantId,xp]` (companion leaderboard), `Clan[tenantId,treasury]` + `Clan[tenantId,warPoints]` (clan + clan-war rankings), `StreamGoal[tenantId,active]` (active-goals reads on the overlay/incrementGoals path), `StreamAlert[tenantId,type,createdAt]` (recent/top-supporters & type-filtered alert reads), `UserCollectible[userId,acquiredAt]` (owned-cards newest-first). Also closes the deferred **#audit-M4 drops** finding: the "first N claimers get the bonus" check was an out-of-transaction `count()` (N racers could all read 0 and all grab the bonus ‚Üí over-minted GT); it's now an **atomic `StreamDrop.claimCount` ordinal** incremented inside the claim transaction (row-locked, so exactly the first `bonusSlots` win). **db push** (additive: 6 indexes + `claimCount Int @default(0)`). Zielone: `tsc`/**392 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **`/market` ‚ÄĒ bound the unbounded reads** **(#560)** ‚ÄĒ the marketplace GET capped active listings (`take: 60`) but loaded the viewer's whole owned-card collection and own listings with no `take`. Added `take: 200` to the owned-card picker (it's the trade selector, not the full collection page ‚ÄĒ generous bound vs. a payload that grows with the catalog) and `take: MAX_ACTIVE_LISTINGS` to the own-listings read (already business-bounded, now defensively too). No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**392 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Semantic search ‚ÄĒ shared (Redis) embeddings + in-flight dedup** **(#559)** ‚ÄĒ the `/search` embeddings (#554) lived in **per-instance `Map`s**, so every cold serverless instance re-embedded the whole corpus, and concurrent first-hits on one instance each fired their own OpenAI batch. Both now go through the shared **`cacheJson`** (Upstash Redis ‚Üí **cross-instance**; per-instance memory fallback when Redis is off): the corpus key carries a content hash (an edited page/achievement/shop item rolls to a fresh key ‚Üí auto re-embed), with TTLs of **6h** (corpus) / **1h** (query). An **in-flight dedup** map coalesces concurrent identical embeds on one instance so a cold start under load fires **one** batch, not N. Dormant/failed embeds throw a sentinel so they're never cached. Fewer OpenAI calls (cost + latency); pure `lib/semantic` unchanged. No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**392 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Twitch EventSub webhook ‚ÄĒ ack-first, process in background** **(#558)** ‚ÄĒ the webhook ran every grant handler + the achievement/season-XP fan-out **synchronously before replying**, so a busy stream (hype-train progress storms, gift-sub bursts) on a **3-connection** DB pool could push the response past Twitch's timeout ‚Üí retries and eventually a **disabled subscription**. Now everything that gates correctness ‚ÄĒ signature + freshness verification and the **idempotency insert** (a retry still loses with P2002) ‚ÄĒ stays synchronous, the tenant is resolved (needs request scope), and then the slow grant/notify/achievement work runs in **`after()`** (Next 16; the platform keeps the function alive via `waitUntil`). Twitch gets a fast 2xx; the background work still completes. Retry/partial-processing semantics are unchanged (handler errors were already swallowed + 200'd). No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**392 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Overlay hot-path caching ‚ÄĒ ~3 fewer DB queries per poll** **(#557)** ‚ÄĒ the OBS overlay SSE feed runs ~1√ó/s **per browser source**, and each tick read alert settings + per-type configs + validated the overlay token = ~3‚Äď4 DB round-trips on a connection pool capped at **3**. Those three reads change only on admin edits, so they now go through the shared **`cacheJson`** (Upstash Redis, cross-instance; in-memory fallback when Redis is off) with short TTLs (settings/type-configs **10s**, token list **30s**). `isValidOverlayToken` caches the token *list* (the constant-time compare stays uncached, so a caller can't poison the cache); `getSettings`/`getAlertTypeConfigs` gained an opt-in `{ cached: true }` used **only** on the overlay hot path ‚ÄĒ admin reads/writes stay live. Token rotation **busts** the cache immediately (new `cacheDelete`) so a re-pasted OBS URL works at once. Per poll the feed drops from ~4 queries to ~1 (the live alert fetch). No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**392 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.

### Code Quality

- **Resolve the React-Compiler ‚ÜĒ ESLint contradiction (audit v3 hygiene)** **(#617)** ‚ÄĒ `next.config` has **`reactCompiler: true`** (the compiler is live), but `eslint.config.mjs` disabled its four correctness rules with a comment claiming *"we don't use the React Compiler"* ‚ÄĒ a misleading config the v3 stack audit flagged as its one genuinely risky spot. Measured the real fallout (turned the rules on: **101 warnings** ‚ÄĒ ~88 `set-state-in-effect` from idiomatic data-fetch effects, plus a few `purity`/`refs` in live-countdown overlays). The compiler **bails out** of optimizing such components rather than miscompiling them, so the app is correct; the rules stay **off** (turning them on + refactoring 101 spots is a separate deliberate sweep, not a build gate) but the **comment is now truthful** about why. No behaviour/schema change. (Routine patch/minor dep bumps intentionally deferred ‚ÄĒ 0 prod vulns, current stack, lockfile/linux-binary risk outweighs marginal gain; the only meaningful version work is `@simplewebauthn` 9‚Üí13, a careful upgrade for the passkey device-test milestone.) Zielone: `tsc`/**431 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Shared `useToast` provider ‚ÄĒ one toast system instead of nine (audit v2)** **(#598)** ‚ÄĒ nine components each re-implemented the same floating-toast feedback (`useState<{kind,msg}>` + a manual `setTimeout` dismissal + a copy-pasted `fixed bottom-6 end-6 ‚Ä¶ shadow-2xl` div with a Check/X icon), with subtly different dismiss timings and **inconsistent or missing `role`/`aria-live`**. New **`lib/`-less `components/ToastProvider`** (mounted once in `Providers`) exposes a `useToast()` hook (`show(kind,msg)` / `ok` / `err`) and renders a single accessible toast stack: correct `role="status"`/`"alert"` + `aria-live` per kind, click-to-dismiss, FIFO-capped at 3, consistent auto-dismiss. Migrated **Shop ¬∑ Admin ¬∑ Predictions ¬∑ Polls ¬∑ Events ¬∑ Seasons ¬∑ Quests ¬∑ Market ¬∑ Collectibles** to it, deleting their local toast state/timers/markup (Admin's OAuth-callback toasts and the per-section `onToast` callback keep working unchanged). Intentionally left the **inline, in-flow** feedback (Clips/Clans/Companion/Portals/Referral/Sounds/Trivia banners + the tiny accent/country/gift/passkey error spans) as-is ‚ÄĒ those render in context by design, not as floating toasts. Net ‚ąí~120 lines of duplication; messages stay caller-localized so the provider is i18n-agnostic. No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**412 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Remove unused Biome tooling (audit v2)** **(#593)** ‚ÄĒ Biome was added (#193) as a complementary lint-only checker but **never wired into CI** (the `quality` job runs ESLint via `npm run lint`), leaving two linters configured but only one enforced ‚ÄĒ dead tooling + an unused dependency. Removed the `lint:biome` script, the `@biomejs/biome` devDependency and `biome.json`; ESLint stays the single source of truth. Lockfile change is biome-only (no other deps touched); `npm audit` still clean. No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**412 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Single-source bet bounds + bounded in-memory cache (audit v2)** **(#578)** ‚ÄĒ the casino games re-inlined the `10` / `100_000` bet bounds (and a triplicated error string) instead of the existing `MIN_BET` / `MAX_BET` in `lib/gt-games`; Mines / Hi-Lo / Blackjack now import them (one source of truth for the bet limits). And the `lib/redis` in-memory cache fallback (used only when Upstash isn't configured) grew unbounded ‚ÄĒ it now FIFO-evicts at **1000** entries so distinct-key churn (per-query overlay/search keys) can't leak memory in a no-Redis/dev setup. No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**412 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.

(2) **11 bare fire-and-forget calls** now carry a defensive `.catch(() => {})` (matching the `notifyStreamLive` convention) so a rejected best-effort side-effect can't surface as an unhandled rejection: `feedJackpot` √ó4 (blackjack/hilo/mines start + double-down), `extendSubathon` √ó6 (Twitch/Kick sub+giftsub, YT super-chat, Streamlabs), `checkGrantAnomaly` √ó1 (admin grant). (3) removed the obsolete `scripts/setup-vapid.mjs` (one-shot VAPID setup; web push is live, keys already on Vercel ‚ÄĒ unreferenced by any script/doc). No schema change. ### Accessibility

- **Enlarge cramped icon-button tap targets (audit v2)** **(#596)** ‚ÄĒ several icon-only buttons were below a comfortable touch size, especially awkward on mobile. The **viewer-facing** ones are now **‚Č•40√ó40px**: the `/profile` social-link save/remove buttons, the `/market` "my listings" cancel button, and the `/support` reveal/copy/QR action buttons (all via `min-w/min-h` or `w-10 h-10` + flex-centering ‚ÄĒ **icon glyphs unchanged**, only the hit area grows). The dense `/admin#goals` row (enable/reset/delete) went 24px‚Üí**36px** ‚ÄĒ a real bump without bloating the admin list. Every enlarged icon button also gained an `aria-label`. Verified the exact rendered dimensions against the live CSS bundle (40/40/36px) and confirmed no row-layout regression. No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**412 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Escape closes the header dropdowns (audit v2)** **(#591)** ‚ÄĒ the theme picker, notification bell and account menu closed on outside-click but not on **Escape**, so keyboard users couldn't dismiss them. Added an Esc-to-close listener to all three (theme + bell extend their existing outside-click effect; the account menu, which used a click backdrop, gets a keydown effect). No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**412 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Bound numeric admin inputs (audit v2)** **(#590)** ‚ÄĒ the shared `FieldInput` accepted `type` but never forwarded `min`/`max`/`step`, so every numeric admin field was unconstrained in-browser. Added the forwarding and applied sensible bounds to the clear-cut fields: drop reward/bonus/slots `min=0`, expiry `min=1`; schedule hour `0‚Äď23`, minute `0‚Äď59`, duration `min=1`. Server-side validation is unchanged ‚ÄĒ this just constrains input at the source. No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**412 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Make the shop-confirm & ranking-admin modals real dialogs (audit v2)** **(#586)** ‚ÄĒ the `/shop` purchase-confirm modal (which spends currency) and the ranking player-admin modal were full-screen overlays with **no `role="dialog"`, no `aria-modal`, no focus management** ‚ÄĒ invisible to screen readers as modals and Tab-leaky. Both now declare `role="dialog"` + `aria-modal="true"` + an `aria-label` (the item / player name) and use the shared **`useFocusTrap`** (focus in, trap Tab, Esc closes when idle, restore focus on close). No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**412 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Focus-trap the admin editor dialogs (audit v2)** **(#585)** ‚ÄĒ the achievement / event / shop-item editor modals declared `role="dialog" aria-modal="true"` but didn't actually trap focus, so keyboard users could Tab into the obscured page behind and there was no Escape-to-close or focus restore (the `aria-modal` was a lie to screen readers). All three now use the shared **`useFocusTrap`** (focus the dialog on open, trap Tab, **Esc closes** when not busy, restore focus to the trigger on close) and their **X close buttons gained an `aria-label`**. No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**412 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Announce admin feedback + make clickable rows real controls (audit v2)** **(#579)** ‚ÄĒ three quick a11y wins: the **admin toast** (`AdminClient`) ‚ÄĒ the primary save/create/delete feedback for the whole panel ‚ÄĒ was a silent `<div>`; it now carries `role="status"`/`aria-live="polite"` (errors `role="alert"`/`assertive`), so screen-reader users hear every outcome. **NotificationItem** (`NotificationBell`) was a clickable `<div>` (unreachable by keyboard for link-less notifications) ‚Üí now a real `<Link>`/`<button>`. **MergeUsers** selection card was a clickable `<div>` ‚Üí now `role="button"` + `tabIndex` + `aria-pressed` + Enter/Space handler. No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**412 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Reusable focus trap + ARIA for the command palette / gift popover / accent picker** **(#564)** ‚ÄĒ the codebase had **no focus-management utility**, so overlays only half-managed focus (focus the input, maybe) and never restored it. New **`lib/use-focus-trap`** hook does the three things a11y needs: on open it moves focus inside (caller's `initialFocus`, else first focusable), while open it **traps Tab/Shift+Tab** inside the container and fires `onEscape`, and on close it **restores focus to the trigger**. Applied to: **CommandPalette** (#548) ‚ÄĒ now a proper combobox/listbox (`role="combobox"` + `aria-expanded`/`aria-controls`/`aria-activedescendant`/`aria-autocomplete` on the input; `role="listbox"` on the results; `role="option"` + `aria-selected` + `tabIndex=-1` on each item) with Esc + focus-restore via the hook (dropping the bespoke focus/Esc code); **GiftButton** (#553) ‚ÄĒ reuses the hook (focus the amount field, trap, Esc, restore), `aria-expanded` on the trigger, localized `aria-label` on the input; **AccentPicker** (#546) ‚ÄĒ the swatch `title`/`aria-label` were the raw English keys ("crimson", ‚Ä¶), now a localized `accentSwatch` string (EN + PL, other locales fall back to EN). No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**401 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.

- **Fix next-intl `INVALID_KEY` from dotted EventSub message keys (audit v2)** **(#597)** ‚ÄĒ the `twitchEventSub.eventType` and `kickEvents.eventLabel` namespaces keyed their labels by the **raw event-type names** (`channel.subscribe`, `channel.subscription.gift`, `livestream.status.updated`, ‚Ä¶). next-intl treats a `.` as a **nesting separator**, so every page render threw `INVALID_KEY: Namespace keys cannot contain the character "."` (~30√ó per load, from `getTranslations` in the locale layout + metadata) and those labels never actually resolved. Renamed the keys to use **underscores** across **all 14 locales** (`channel_subscribe`, ‚Ä¶); the two readers (`TwitchEventSubManager`, `KickEvents`) now map the dotted runtime event type to the underscored key via a tiny `type.replace(/\./g, "_")` helper, falling back to the raw type. Data + two call sites; no behaviour change beyond the labels now resolving and the error log going quiet. Key parity preserved (2886/2886). No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**412 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.

- **Daily-task claim ‚ÄĒ check the response, soft-refresh, retry on failure (audit v2)** **(#581)** ‚ÄĒ the home "daily task" claim button `fetch`ed `/api/tasks/claim` and then **unconditionally `window.location.reload()`d**, so a failed claim looked exactly like success and the whole page hard-reloaded. It now checks `res.ok`, does a soft **`router.refresh()`** on success, and **re-enables the button on failure** (so the viewer can retry) with a busy-disabled state in between. No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**412 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Error vs. empty ‚ÄĒ stop showing a fake "nothing here" on a failed fetch (audit v2)** **(#580)** ‚ÄĒ six client pages caught load failures with `catch { /* leave empty */ }`, so a **network error rendered the same "nothing here yet" empty state** (looks broken, no recovery). `/clips`, `/sounds`, `/trivia`, `/portals` now track an error flag and render the shared **`ErrorState` with a Retry button** on failure (distinct from a genuine empty list); `/companion` and `/clans` (which showed a bare error line) now use the same `ErrorState` + retry. Localized via the shared `common.errorTitle`/`common.retry`. No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**412 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Marketplace feedback ‚ÄĒ buy confirmation + auto-dismissing toasts** **(#566)** ‚ÄĒ `/market` actions reported via a **sticky amber banner** with no positive confirmation. Now buying first asks a **confirmation** ("Buy {card} for {price}?") so a stray tap can't spend GT, and every action lands a **toast that auto-dismisses after ~3.2s** ‚ÄĒ **emerald** on success (`bought`/`listed`/`cancelled`) and **red** on error (the localized `err_*` message) ‚ÄĒ replacing the amber banner. The toast is `role="status"` `aria-live="polite"`. EN + PL (others fall back to EN). No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**401 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Shared `EmptyState` / `ErrorState` across collectibles ¬∑ market ¬∑ search ¬∑ support** **(#565)** ‚ÄĒ these four pages each hand-rolled their own "nothing here yet" markup (slightly different padding/borders), and two also rendered a bare one-line load error. They now use the existing shared **`EmptyState`** (branded block + themed icon, fully localized via each page's `empty`/`noCards`/`noListings` keys) and **`ErrorState`** (collectibles + market load failures ‚Üí a retry-able error block). `ErrorState` gained optional `title`/`retryLabel` props (Polish defaults preserved for the existing admin caller) so the new call sites can localize ‚ÄĒ added generic `common.errorTitle` / `common.retry` (EN + PL). Removed Market's local `Empty` helper. Consistent look + a retry path where there was none. No schema change. Zielone: `tsc`/**401 test√≥w**/`eslint`/`build`.
- **Make `/support` discoverable** **(#520)** ‚ÄĒ added a "‚ô• Support" link in the site footer (every page) and taught the help assistant about `/support`, so viewers can actually find the new tip page from inside the portal (not only via a shared link). No schema change.

Streamer-only re-consent; viewers' login OAuth is separate and unaffected.

- **GT sound redemptions ‚ÄĒ spend GT to play a sound on stream** **(#505)** ‚ÄĒ viewers spend %gt% to play a streamer-curated sound live on the OBS alerts overlay. ### Security

- **Rate-limit per-IP na publicznych GET-ach (z roadmapy ¬ß4)** **(#486)** ‚ÄĒ istniejńÖca infra per-IP (Redis + fallback DB) chroniŇāa publiczne POST-y (award/telemetry); rozszerzona na niezabezpieczone publiczne odczyty bijńÖce w bazńô: `/api/games` (60/min/IP ‚ÄĒ biblioteka gier), `/api/gt-games/jackpot` (120/min ‚ÄĒ pollowane przez UI kasyna), `/api/health` (120/min ‚ÄĒ ochrona maŇāego poolera; nadal poprawnie raportuje `db:down`, bo limiter fail-open przy bŇāńôdzie DB). Ten sam wzorzec `extractIp`+`rateLimit`+`rateLimitHeaders(429)` co w award (czyta jak reszta kodu, zero nowej abstrakcji). Zielone: `tsc`/261/`eslint`/`build`.

### Performance

- **Rate-limit: szybka ŇõcieŇľka Redis (atomowy INCR) z fallbackiem do DB (audyt #453, #1 perf-finding chat-award)** ‚ÄĒ limiter robiŇā **2 zapytania Postgres** (findUnique + update/create) na kaŇľde sprawdzenie, a chat-award sprawdza 2√ó ‚Üí **4 zapytania/wiadomoŇõńá** przez maŇāy pooler. Teraz preferuje Redis (Upstash): jeden atomowy `INCR`+`PEXPIRE` przez skrypt Lua (bez wyŇõcigu incr/expire). **BezpieczeŇĄstwo zachowania:** bez Redisa ‚Üí ŇõcieŇľka DB (bez zmian); bŇāńÖd Redisa ‚Üí degradacja do **sprawdzonej ŇõcieŇľki DB** (nie prosto do fail-open); guard ksztaŇātu wyniku `eval` (malformed ‚Üí fallback, nie liczenie na `undefined`); obie ŇõcieŇľki fail-open na wŇāasnym bŇāńôdzie (nigdy nie blokujńÖ legitnego ruchu). ŇöcieŇľka DB wyodrńôbniona do `rateLimitDb` bez zmian logiki. Zielone: `tsc`/**234 testy**/`build` (ŇõcieŇľka Redis aktywna tylko na prodzie z Upstash).

- **Daily-tasks: cache katalogu zadaŇĄ w hot-path nagr√≥d (audyt #452)** ‚ÄĒ `updateDailyTaskProgress` (woŇāane per nagrodzona wiadomoŇõńá czatu/Discorda) robiŇāo `findMany` aktywnych zadaŇĄ **co wywoŇāanie**, mimo Ňľe katalog zadaŇĄ jest w runtime statyczny (seedowany, Ňľadna trasa go nie mutuje). Cache listy id per `triggerType` (~5 min) + early-return gdy brak zadaŇĄ danego typu (pomija pńôtlńô upsert√≥w caŇākowicie) + `today()` policzony raz zamiast 3√ó w pńôtli. Zielone: `tsc`/**234 testy**/`build`.

- **Sezon: cache w hot-path nagr√≥d (audyt #450)** ‚ÄĒ `getOrCreateCurrentSeason()` robiŇā `updateMany` (WRITE ‚Äědeaktywuj wygasŇāe") + `findUnique` na **kaŇľde** wywoŇāanie ‚ÄĒ w tym ŇõcieŇľkńô nagr√≥d czatu (per wiadomoŇõńá). Sezon jest globalny (jeden wiersz/`number` miesińÖca) i zmienia sińô raz w miesińÖcu ‚Üí cache in-process ~5 min (jedyna nieŇõwieŇľoŇõńá: kilka minut na przeŇāomie miesińÖca, kosmetyczna ‚ÄĒ XP lńÖduje na serwowanym id sezonu); `invalidateSeasonCache()` wpińôte w admin `update_season`, by edycja widańá byŇāo od razu. Zielone: `tsc`/**234 testy**/`build`.

- **i18n: memoizacja zmergowanego katalogu per locale (audyt #449)** ‚ÄĒ `deepMerge(en, localized)` (~2200 kluczy, fallback brakujńÖcych tŇāumaczeŇĄ do EN) liczyŇā sińô na **kaŇľde ŇľńÖdanie** ZANIM cache `brandedMessages` m√≥gŇā zadziaŇāańá (cache'uje tylko wynik podmiany brandingu, nie wejŇõcie). Teraz katalog jest memoizowany raz per locale (‚Č§14 wpis√≥w, statyczny JSON nie zmienia sińô w runtime); zachowana semantyka `brandKey` (locale brakujńÖce/EN dzielńÖ klucz cache brandingu ‚Äěen"). Mniej pracy CPU na render kaŇľdej strony pod force-dynamic. Zachowanie 1:1. Zielone: `tsc`/**234 testy**/`build`.

### Changed

- **Sp√≥jnoŇõńá: konsolidacja 11 tras alert√≥w w 1 dynamicznńÖ + kasacja martwego scaffoldu (audyt P2 #448)** ‚ÄĒ dŇāug sp√≥jnoŇõci z audytu architektury: **11 niemal identycznych tras** `/api/alerts/{goals,subathon,polls,predictions,recent-events,emoji-combo,rumble,wheel,widget,chat,viewers}` (kaŇľda ~21 linii r√≥ŇľnińÖcych sińô jednym kluczem `OVERLAY_FEEDS.<x>`) ‚Üí **jedna `/api/alerts/[feed]`** (`getOverlayFeed(feed)` + 404 dla nieznanego); URL-e OBS bez zmian (Next preferuje statyczne `queue`/`stream`, dynamiczna Ňāapie resztńô ‚ÄĒ smoke: stare ŇõcieŇľki dalej 401 bez tokenu, nieznany feed 404). Zielone: `tsc`/`build`/smoke.

- **Bot czatu: odpornoŇõńá na padnińôcia + higiena (audyt #447)** ‚ÄĒ poprawki ze ŇõcieŇľki-poraŇľki (hot-path sukcesu bez zmian): Kick reconnect ze **staŇāych 5s ‚Üí exponential backoff + jitter** (resetowany przy udanym poŇāńÖczeniu ‚ÄĒ koniec Ňāomotania martwego endpointu); **retry startowy** lookupu chatroom-id Kicka (3√ó/10s ‚ÄĒ transientny Cloudflare-gate przy boot zabijaŇā Kicka na caŇāe Ňľycie procesu) i pierwszego tokenu YouTube (3√ó/15s); mapa `offenders` eskalacji moderacji **prune'owana** (rosŇāa bez koŇĄca przez caŇāy uptime ‚ÄĒ teraz wpisy poza oknem 30 min sńÖ usuwane); `.env.example` dopisane brakujńÖce `TWITCH_BOT_REFRESH`/`KICK_TOKEN_STORE`/`YT_AUTH_REDIRECT`. **‚ö†ÔłŹ aktywne po restarcie bota na `main`.** *(Ňöwiadomie ODŇĀOŇĽONE: migracja automoda Twitch z martwych komend IRC tmi.js `delete`/`timeout` na Helix moderation API ‚ÄĒ wymaga re-auth bota z nowymi scope'ami `moderator:manage:*` + weryfikacji na Ňľywym kanale; osobny krok z udziaŇāem usera, by nie wciskańá nietestowalnego kodu w hot-path.)* Bot `tsc` czysty.

- **Hardening CI przed powrotem Actions (audyt #446)** ‚ÄĒ punkty ‚Äězgnicia" wskazane przez audyt narzńôdzi (GH Actions czekajńÖ na odblokowanie billingu konta ‚ÄĒ niech wr√≥cńÖ zdrowe): `e2e-smoke.yml` (dzienny smoke prod) podbity z `actions/checkout@v4`+`setup-node@v4` ‚Üí **v6** (sp√≥jnie z `ci.yml`) i `playwright install --with-deps` ‚Üí samo `chromium` (apt-get update cińÖgnńÖŇā flaky repo Google Chrome ‚ÄĒ ubuntu-latest ma juŇľ biblioteki Chromium); `ci.yml` `npm install` ‚Üí **`npm ci`** w 3 jobach (lockfile zsynchronizowany po #445 ‚ÄĒ `npm ci` Ňāapie dryf package.json‚ÜĒlock, kt√≥rego `npm install` by nie pokazaŇā); dodane `engines.node >=22` (dokumentuje wersjńô, adresuje rozjazd CI-22/lokalnie-26). Bez zmian w kodzie aplikacji. Lokalnie: `tsc`/**242 testy**/`build` zielone.
